YES

********************************************************************************
Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Reversing the system.
Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 9-rules system (6 strict rules).
Removing 2 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 7-rules system (4 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 88-rules system (16 strict rules).
Removing 3 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 85-rules system (16 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 81-rules system (16 strict rules).
Removing 4 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 77-rules system (16 strict rules).
Removing 9 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 68-rules system (11 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 64-rules system (11 strict rules).
Removing 4 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 60-rules system (11 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 972-rules system (47 strict rules).
Removing 43 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 929-rules system (47 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TROCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 865-rules system (47 strict rules).
Removing 64 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 801-rules system (47 strict rules).
Removing 394 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 407-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED

Proof:

After renaming modulo the bijection { a ↦ 0, b ↦ 1, c ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 1 ⟶ ,
  1 2 ⟶ 0 0 ,
  2 0 ⟶ 1 1 2 2 }

Reversing the system.
After renaming modulo the bijection { 1 ↦ 0, 0 ↦ 1, 2 ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 1 ⟶ ,
  2 0 ⟶ 1 1 ,
  1 2 ⟶ 2 2 0 0 }

Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
  Here, ↑ marks so-called defined symbols.
After renaming modulo the bijection { (2,↑) ↦ 0, (0,↓) ↦ 1, (1,↑) ↦ 2, (1,↓) ↦ 3, (2,↓) ↦ 4, (0,↑) ↦ 5 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 9-rules system (6 strict rules)
{ 0 1 ⟶ 2 3 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 2 ,
  2 4 ⟶ 0 4 1 1 ,
  2 4 ⟶ 0 1 1 ,
  2 4 ⟶ 5 1 ,
  2 4 ⟶ 5 ,
  1 3 →= ,
  4 1 →= 3 3 ,
  3 4 →= 4 4 1 1 }
